                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`

                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0

                                ,c.use_sales
                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email

                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0

                                ,c.use_hierarchy
                                ,c.use_delivery
                                ,c.use_msgkey
                                ,c.temp_sensors
                                ,c.use_portable
                                ,c.use_buzzer
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_freeze
                                ,c.use_door_sensor
                                ,c.use_ac_sensor
                                ,c.use_genset_sensor
                                ,c.use_fuel_sensor
                                ,c.use_routing
                                ,c.use_advanced_alert
                                ,c.use_panic
                                ,c.use_mobility
                                ,c.use_secondary_sales
                                ,c.use_sales
                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,c.use_secondary_sales
                                ,c.use_sales
                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0

                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0

                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,c.use_routing

                                ,c.use_panic
                                ,c.use_mobility
                                ,c.use_secondary_sales
                                ,c.use_sales
                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,c.use_humidity

                                ,c.use_toggle_switch

                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0

                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1

                                ,u.panic_telephone
                                ,u.panic_mobilenotification
                                ,u.immob_sms
                                ,u.immob_email
                                ,u.immob_telephone
                                ,u.immob_mobilenotification
                                ,u.door_sms
                                ,u.door_email
                                ,u.door_telephone
                                ,u.door_mobilenotification
                                ,u.delivery_vehicleid
                                ,u.tempinterval
                                ,u.igninterval
                                ,u.speedinterval
                                ,u.acinterval
                                ,u.doorinterval
                                ,u.hum_sms
                                ,u.hum_email
                                ,u.hum_telephone
                                ,u.hum_mobilenotification
                                ,u.huminterval
                                ,u.vehicle_movement_alert
                                ,u.refreshtime
                                ,u.customerno
                                ,u.isdeleted
                                ,u.isTempInrangeAlertRequired
                                ,u.isAdvTempConfRange
                                ,c.use_tracking
                                ,c.maintenance_limit
                                ,c.use_maintenance
                                ,c.use_hierarchy
                                ,c.use_delivery
                                ,c.use_msgkey
                                ,c.temp_sensors
                                ,c.use_portable
                                ,c.use_buzzer
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_freeze
                                ,c.use_door_sensor
                                ,c.use_ac_sensor
                                ,c.use_genset_sensor
                                ,c.use_fuel_sensor
                                ,c.use_routing
                                ,c.use_advanced_alert
                                ,c.use_panic
                                ,c.use_mobility
                                ,c.use_secondary_sales
                                ,c.use_sales
                                ,c.use_tms
                                ,c.use_immobiliser
                                ,c.use_extradigital
                                ,c.use_warehouse
                                ,c.use_pickup
                                ,c.use_trip
                                ,c.use_humidity
                                ,c.timezone
                                ,c.use_toggle_switch
                                ,c.multiauth
                                ,c.use_elixiadoc
                                ,c.rel_manager
                                ,c.isoffline
                                ,rm.manager_name
                                ,rm.manager_email
                                ,rm.manager_mobile
                                ,tri.`interval` as trinterval
                                ,veh.`interval` as vehinterval
                                ,setting.`use_location_summary`
                                ,setting.`use_vehicle_type`
                                ,setting.`use_checkpoint_settings`
                                ,timezone.timediff
                                ,timezone.timezone as timezonename
                                ,g.groupname
                        FROM    `user` u
                        INNER JOIN speed.customer c ON c.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT JOIN speed.relationship_manager rm on rm.rid = c.rel_manager
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`tempreportinterval` as tri on tri.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`vehrepinterval` as veh on veh.userid = u.userid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`setting` ON setting.customerno = u.customerno
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`timezone` ON c.timezone = timezone.tid
                        LEFT OUTER JOIN speed.`group` g ON u.groupid = g.groupid AND u.groupid != 0 and g.customerno = u.customerno
                        WHERE   u.customerno=132
                        AND     u.userid='567'
                        AND     u.isdeleted=0
                        AND     c.isoffline = 0
                        LIMIT   1
